OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add = {
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add"
	#历史折线图的时间存储器 玩家桑~泥也不希望折线图看不到时间罢
	add_to_array = {
		global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates = global.date
		index = 0
	}
}

#宣战
OCF_After_collapse_government_Declare_war = {
	every_other_country = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PREV
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = EIA
				is_core_of = INP
				is_core_of = OFC
				is_core_of = KEZ
				is_core_of = SIE
				is_core_of = FLA
				is_core_of = KCL
				is_core_of = KGF
				is_core_of = ROM
				is_core_of = TKD
				is_core_of = GFZ
				is_core_of = BRI
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
			}
			add_state_core = PREV
		}
	}
}

#内战结束
OCF_end_of_civil_war = {
	OCF = {
		remove_from_array = {
			global.has_ruling_coalition = THIS
		}
		OCF_eliminate_current_ruling_party = yes
		OCF_clear_all_deputy_leaders = yes
		set_country_flag = OCF_abolition_parliament_yes_flag
		transfer_state = 115
		add_state_core = 115
		inherit_technology = ROOT
		set_variable = {
			OCF_bill = 150
		}
		country_event = {
			id = OCF.2
			days = 4			#回收海雾舰队
		}
		load_focus_tree = NO_focus_tree		#载入空国策，以后判断载入什么
	}
	ROOT = {
		#转移所有海军 会有海军吗？
		transfer_navy = {
			target = OCF
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		#吞并其余势力
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
			NOT = {
				tag = ROOT
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PREV
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			set_nationality = OCF
		}
	}
	ROOT = {
		#吞并所有将领
		every_unit_leader = {
			set_nationality = OCF
		}
	}
	if = {
		#一下就是各种检测战胜国，这注释我就不写了
		limit = {
			tag = INP
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
			}
			set_nationality = {
				target_country = OCF
				character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = INP_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
			}
			set_nationality = {
				target_country = OCF
				character = INP_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
			}
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = INP_unification
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 1
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = INP_fascism_party_2_long
				name = INP_fascism_party_2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = INP_democratic_party_2_long
				name = INP_democratic_party_2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = INP_communism_party_long
				name = INP_communism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = INP_neutrality_party_long
				name = INP_neutrality_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = reactionism
				long_name = INP_reactionism_party_long
				name = INP_reactionism_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
				ideology = sub_Regressivism
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
				ideology = sub_Facism
			}
			add_ideas = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = OFC
				tag = KEZ
				tag = SIE
				tag = KCL
				tag = KGF
				tag = BRI
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TAG = KEZ
			}
			set_global_flag = OCF_civil_war_so_it_was_unified_flag_KEZ
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = OCF_fourth
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			tag = TKD
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = TKD_kingdom
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			tag = GFZ
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GFZ_unification
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = regions_belonging_OCF_flag
		}
		remove_core_of = ANA
		remove_core_of = OFC
		remove_core_of = KEZ
		remove_core_of = SIE
		remove_core_of = FLA
		remove_core_of = KCL
		remove_core_of = KGF
		remove_core_of = ROM
		remove_core_of = TKD
		remove_core_of = GFZ
		remove_core_of = BRI
		remove_core_of = INP
		remove_core_of = EIA
		add_core_of = OCF
		transfer_state_to = OCF
	}
}

	}
}

#崩溃的政府体系计算
OCF_collapsed_government_system_yes = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
		}
		remove_ideas = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_7
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_collapsed_government_system_7
	}
}

OCF_Random_infrastructure = {
	#随机给个基建
	random_owned_controlled_state = {
		limit = {
			free_building_slots = {
				building = infrastructure
				size > 0
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_home_area = yes
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						any_owned_state = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = infrastructure
								size > 0
							}
							is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_building_construction = {
			type = infrastructure
			level = 1
			instant_build = yes
		}
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
	}
}

#军工
OCF_Randomly_give_military_industry = {
	random_owned_controlled_state = {
		limit = {
			free_building_slots = {
				building = arms_factory
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_home_area = yes
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						any_owned_state = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
							is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		add_building_construction = {
			type = arms_factory
			level = 1
			instant_build = yes
		}
	}
}

								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
							is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
				}

		}
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1

			level = 1

		}
	}

	}

}

#联邦放映公司更新

	set_variable = {
		OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = OCF_poster_iconType_variable_2
	}
	OCF_federal_film_company_initialization_variable = yes
	set_variable = {
		OCF_poster_iconType_variable_2 = variable
	}
	OCF_federal_film_company_bonus = yes
}

#设置加成
OCF_federal_film_company_bonus = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_stability_factor = 0
	}
	#稳定
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_factory = 0
	}
	#产出
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0
	}
	#船坞
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0
	}
	#科研
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0
	}
	#建造
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_army_attack_factor = 0
	}
	#攻击
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.07
		}
	}
	#幸运星
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0.05
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_factory = 0.03
		}
	}
	#石之门
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 6
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_stability_factor = 0.1
		}
	}
	#猫咪日常
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 7
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0.12
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_stability_factor = -0.08
		}
	}
	#快要坏掉的八音盒
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 8
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0.1
		}
	}
	#苍蓝钢铁
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 9
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0.08
		}
	}
	#笨拙至极的上野
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 10
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_army_attack_factor = 0.07
		}
	}
	#爱杀宝贝
}

#初始化工坊
OCF_initialize_workshop = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization = OCF.weapon_reliability
	}
	#武器可靠性优化程度
	set_variable = {
		OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization = OCF.weapon_kill
	}
	#武器可用性优化程度
	set_variable = {
		OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure = OCF.weapon_structure
	}
	#当前武器结构性优化程度
	clr_country_flag = OCF_entrusting_grand_chancellor_flag	#去除大执政官标记
}

#每周工坊数值增加
OCF_workshop_values_increase = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_reliability_increase = OCF.weapon_reliability_increase_add
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_reliability_increase = modifier@ocf_weapon_reliability_correct
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_kill_increase = OCF.weapon_kill_increase_add
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_kill_increase = modifier@ocf_weapon_kill_correct
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_structure_increase = OCF.weapon_structure_increase_add
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_structure_increase = modifier@ocf_weapon_structure_correct
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_reliability_progress = OCF.weapon_reliability_increase
	}
	#武器可靠性
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_kill_progress = OCF.weapon_kill_increase
	}
	#武器杀伤
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_structure_progress = OCF.weapon_structure_increase
	}
	#武器结构
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_reliability_progress > 100
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_reliability = 1
		}
		#可靠
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.weapon_reliability > 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_reliability = 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_reliability_progress = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_kill_progress > 100
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_kill = 1
		}
		#杀伤
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.weapon_kill > 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_kill = 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_kill_progress = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_structure_progress > 100
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_structure = 1
		}
		#结构
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.weapon_structure > 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_structure = 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_structure_progress = 0
		}
	}
}

#防止工坊数值溢出
OCF_prevent_overflow_of_workshop_values = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization > 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization = 100
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization > 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization = 100
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure > 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure = 100
		}
	}
}

#判定工坊结果
OCF_judging_workshop_results = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization
	}
	#先算一下平均值
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = 3
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_5 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>99
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_10 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>89
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_9 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>79
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_8 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>69
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_7 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>59
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_6 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>49
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_5 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>39
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_4 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>29
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>19
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_2 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>9
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_1 = yes
	}
	else = {
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_0 = yes
	}
}

#科技修正添加
#扩编工程兵团
enable_ocf_expanded_engineer_corps = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = {
			localization_key = tooltip_enable_hidden_tech
			TECH = country_culture|ocf_expanded_engineer_corps
			EFFECT = tech_effect|ocf_expanded_engineer_corps
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_expanded_engineer_corps = 1
			popup = no
		}
	}
}

#扩编海军陆战队
enable_ocf_expand_marine_corps = {

#初始化资金调整
set_custom_slider = {
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			slider_buttons = val
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			OCF_adjusting_military_spending_buttons = val
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			OCF_adjusting_education_expenses_buttons = val
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			OCF_adjusting_medical_treatment_buttons = val
		}
	}
}

##资金获取（效果预估）
OCF_obtain_banknotes_effect_estimation = {
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = current_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = -0.1
	}
	#计算修正（抬高税收稳定度修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = 0.004
	}
	#获取民用工厂
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ROOT.num_of_civilian_factories
	}
	#计算修正（民用工厂税收贡献修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2
	}
	#获取稳定度
	set_variable = {
		OCF_stability_variable_30 = ROOT.stability
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_stability_variable_30 < 0.3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_stability_variable_30 = 0.3
		}
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
	}
	#税收基础值
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact = current_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = 0.1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = tax_impact
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
	}
	#计算修正（税收修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2
	}
	OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_estimate = yes
	set_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = 2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
		}
		#获取战争支持
		set_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
		}
		divide_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 500
		}
		#军队花费
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}
		#计算修正（军费开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
		}
		#计算修正（军费战时开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2
		}
		#减去军队花费
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
		}
		#获取战争支持
		set_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
		}
		divide_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1200
		}
		#军队花费
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}
		#计算修正（军费开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
		}
		#计算修正（军费维护开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2
		}
		#减去军队花费
	}
	#军费修正
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_military_spending_int
	}
	set_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = adjusting_military_spending_int
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = -20
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = 0.2
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = 0.025
	}
	#教育修正
	set_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = adjusting_education_expenses_int
	}
	#计算修正（教育开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_education_expenses_int_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = adjusting_education_expenses_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = 0.2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = 0
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = 0.02
	}
	#医疗修正
	set_variable = {
		adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2 = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
	}
	#计算修正（医疗开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = -7.5
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = 0.2
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = 0.05
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0.1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
	}
	#计算修正（资金总开支修正）
	set_variable = {

	}
	add_to_variable = {

	}

		OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2
	}

#资金（ 获取资金）
OCF_obtain_banknotes = {
	#获取民用工厂
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ROOT.num_of_civilian_factories
	}
	#计算修正（民用工厂税收贡献修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2
	}
	#获取稳定度
	set_variable = {
		OCF_stability_variable_30 = ROOT.stability
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_stability_variable_30 < 0.3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_stability_variable_30 = 0.3
		}
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
	}
	#税收基础值
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact = current_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = 0.1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = tax_impact
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
	}
	#计算修正（税收修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact = current_int
	}
	#显示的稳定度下降
	add_to_variable = {
		tax_impact = 0
	}
	#废弃
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = -0.1
	}
	#计算修正（抬高税收稳定度修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact_100 = tax_impact
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_100 = 0.004
	}
	#加成数值
	OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold = yes
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_bill = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable
	}
	if = {
		#AI的每月额外资金(他都是AI了你就让着他呗 >_<||| )
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_bill = 30
		}
	}
	OCF_spending_funds = yes
}

#获取资金阈值（预估）
OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_estimate = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = 70		#这里就是基础值
	}
	#计算修正（税收上限修正）
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = modifier@ocf_tax_cap_correction
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable > OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable < 2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = 2
		}
	}
}

#获取资金阈值
OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = 70
	}
	#计算修正（税收上限修正）
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = modifier@ocf_tax_cap_correction
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable > OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable < 2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = 2
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_bill = modifier@ocf_capital_monthly_additional_funds
	}
}

#花费资金
OCF_spending_funds = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = 2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
		}
		#获取战争支持
		set_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
		}
		divide_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 500
		}
		#军队花费
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}

		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2

	else = {

		}

		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}
		#计算修正（军费开支修正）

#检测每月收入
OCF_check_monthly_income = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		OCF_check_monthly_income_temp = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		OCF_check_monthly_income_temp = modifier@ocf_capital_monthly_additional_funds
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		OCF_check_monthly_income_temp = OCF_spending_funds_variable
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		alert_id = token:alert_OCF_Income_deficit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_check_monthly_income_temp < 0
			}
		}
		add_IRIS_alert_unless_exists = yes
	}
	else = {
		del_IRIS_alert = yes
	}
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission OCF_check_monthly_income 检测每月收入：[?OCF_check_monthly_income_temp]"
}

		}
		10 = {

				factor = 1.2
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_senate_yes > 40
				}
			}

				}

			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_senate_no_add = yes
		}
		5 = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_senate_yes > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_senate_yes > 60
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_senate_yes > 80
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = OCE_Rub_cards_new_4
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_senate_yes_del = yes
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_senate_no_add = yes
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_senate_yes_del = yes
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_senate_no_add = yes
		}
		5 = {

				}
			}

#添加可通过议案
OCF_proposal_can_passed_add = {
	add_to_variable = {
		ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed = 1
	}
	OCF_proposal_can_passed_add_sign = yes
}

#移除可通过议案
OCF_proposal_can_passed_del = {
	add_to_variable = {
		ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed = -1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed < 0
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed < 1
			}
		}
		OCF_proposal_can_passed_del_sign = yes
	}
}

#添加可通过议案-标识
OCF_proposal_can_passed_add_sign = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		alert_id = token:alert_OCF_proposal_passed
	}
	add_IRIS_alert_unless_exists = yes
}

#移除可通过议案-标识
OCF_proposal_can_passed_del_sign = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		alert_id = token:alert_OCF_proposal_passed
	}
	del_IRIS_alert = yes
}

					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_1 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_2 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_2 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_3 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_3 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_4 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_4 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_5 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_5 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_6 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_6 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_7 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_7 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_8 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_8 = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	OCF_Insert_Party_Position = yes
}

#裁员到600
OCF_Layoffs_automatic = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_gridbox_seat_array_6 > 600
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			OCF_Layoffs_automatic = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_6
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			OCF_Layoffs_automatic = -600
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = OCF_Layoffs_automatic
			OCF_Layoffs = yes
		}
	}
}

#计算政府影响力
OCF_calculate_government_influence = {
	if = {
		#大洋社会主义同盟
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_1
		}
	}
	if = {

		}

		}

#政府权威性
OCF_government_authority = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_6
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_8
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = 0.64
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning_100 = 0.12
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning = OCF_federal_government_max_planning_100
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed_100 = 0.18
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed = OCF_federal_government_planning_speed_100
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed_100 = 0.08
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed = OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed_100
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_political_power_factor_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_political_power_factor_100 = 0.3
	}
	set_variable = {

	}

##    ##  ##       ##       ##    ##  ##       ##    ## ##     ##    ##    ##  ##       ##    ##   ##  ##     ## ##   ### ##     ## ##          ##    ## ##     ## ##        ##        ##     ## ##    ##     ##       ##    ##  ##     ##    ##    ##
##     ## ######## ##       ##     ## ########  ######  ##     ##    ##     ## ########  ######   ####  #######  ##    ## ##     ## ########     ######   #######  ##        ##         #######  ##     ##    ##       ##     ## ##     ##    ##    ########
#输入变量 pie_chart_angle 角度
#输出变量 coordinate_x x坐标
OCF_calculation_x_position = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				pie_chart_angle > 180
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 1
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = 7
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = up_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s = 50000
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s = down_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_x = up_s
	}
	divide_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_x = down_s
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				decreased = 1
			}
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			coordinate_x = -1
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 0
		}
	}
}

#输入变量 pie_chart_angle 角度
#输出变量 coordinate_y y坐标
OCF_calculation_y_position = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		angle_init = pie_chart_angle
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = 90
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				pie_chart_angle > 180
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				pie_chart_angle > 180
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 0
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = 7
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = up_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s = 50000
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s = down_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = up_s
	}
	divide_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = down_s
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				decreased = 1
			}
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			coordinate_y = -1
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 0
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = angle_init
	}
}

#饼图百分比坐标刷新
OCF_refresh_pie_chart_percentage_coordinates = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = factions_region_1
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = 3.4
	}
	OCF_calculation_x_position = yes
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_x = 30
	}
	set_variable = {
		coordinate_x_1 = coordinate_x
	}
	OCF_calculation_y_position = yes
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = -30
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = 60
	}
	set_variable = {
		coordinate_y_1 = coordinate_y
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = factions_region_2
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {

#刷新全国支持率
OCF_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correctionresh_national_support_rate = {
	OCF = {
		OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_1 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_2 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_3 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_4 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_5 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_6 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_7 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_8 = 0
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_votable_areas_triggers = yes
		}
		OCF = {
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_1 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_2 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_3 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_4 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_5 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_6 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_7 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_8 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
			}
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_2
	}

		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_6
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_8
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_1_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_1
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_2_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_3_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_3
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_4_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_4
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_5_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_5
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_6_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_6
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_7_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_7
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_8_proportion = OCF.OCF_national_support_8
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_1_proportion = OCF_national_support_all
	}
	divide_variable = {

#刷新地区支持率
OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = {
	OCF = {
		OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
	}
	#读取该地区每个党派数量算总数
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
	}
	#保留原数据
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate_100 = THIS.regional_support_rate
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate_100 = 0.01
	}
	#计算占比
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	#把数据传入后端， 显示饼图
	OCF = {
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_1 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_1
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_2 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_2
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_3 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_3
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_4 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_4
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_5 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_5
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_6 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_6
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_7 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_7
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region_8 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion_8
		}
		#储存真实百分比
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_1_storage
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_2_storage
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_3_storage
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_4_storage
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_5_storage
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_6_storage
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_7_storage
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_8_storage
		}
	}
	#计算当前最高值和计算可能胜选党派
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 = 0
	}
	#初始化各个党派
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 2
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 3
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 4
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 5
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 6
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 7
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 1
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 = 1
		}
	}
	#计算可能胜出党派
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 0
	}
	#胜选派
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max = 0
	}
	#最大胜选派
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 6
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 7
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 8
		}
	}
	OCF_government_authority = yes
	OCF = {
		OCF_refresh_pie_chart_percentage_coordinates = yes
	}
}

#刷新可能获胜党派(暂时废弃)
OCF_Refreshing_possible_winning_parties = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_votable_areas_triggers = yes
		}
	}
}

#临时大选代码
OCF_election_results = {
	OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = has_OCF_101_flag
		}
		country_event = {
			id = OCF.25
			days = 5
		}
	}
	else = {
		country_event = {
			id = OCF.101
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

#计算获胜使用
OCF_calculate_winning_usage = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_1 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_2 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_3 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_4 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_5 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_6 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_7 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_8 = 0
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_votable_areas_triggers = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 6
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 8
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 1
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_1 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 2
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_2 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 3
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_3 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 4
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_4 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 5
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_5 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 6
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_6 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 7
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_7 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 8
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_8 = 1
			}
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_1
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_2 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 2
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_3 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 3
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_4 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 4
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_5 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 5
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_6 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 6
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_6
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_7 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 7
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_7
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_8 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_8
		}
	}
}

#调整至100值
OCF_region_supports_formatting = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OCF_computable_region_triggers = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8
			}
			#如果超过100
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						THIS.temp > 100
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					THIS.temp = -100
				}
				for_loop_effect = {
					end = THIS.temp
					random_list = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8 = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			#如果小于100
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						THIS.temp < 100
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					THIS.temp = -100
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					THIS.temp = -1
				}
				for_loop_effect = {
					end = THIS.temp
					random_list = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8 = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#打压党派
OCF_suppress_political_parties = {
	OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = yes
	OCF_Prevent_spillage = yes
	OCF = {
		OCF_government_authority = yes
		OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
		OCF_region_supports_formatting = yes
	}
}

OCF_suppress_political_parties_1 = {
	OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1_del = yes
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_changes_party_relations
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_reduce_relationships_I_3
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			state = ROOT.OCF_select_region_variable
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_Party_TT_6_2_1_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = -35
		}
		add_to_array = {
			global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_change_record_array = 25
			index = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 < 0
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = 0
			}
		}
		OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add = yes
		OCF_suppress_political_parties = yes
	}
}

			state = ROOT.OCF_select_region_variable
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_Party_TT_6_2_7_tt

			index = 0
		}

	}

		}
		add_to_array = {
			global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_change_record_array = 1
			index = 0
		}
		OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add = yes

#增加党派地区支持度
#接受临时变量
#factions_temp 派系
#seat_temp 席位

#弃用代码
OCF_increase_support_for_political_parties_regions = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						seat_temp < 0
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp > -15
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp > -30
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_2
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp > -45
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_3
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_4
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 10
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_0
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 25
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 40
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_2
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 55
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_3
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_4
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = OCF_increase_support_for_political_parties_regions_tt
				INDENTATION = ""
				ICON = "[?temp_icon.GetTokenLocalizedKey]"
				FACTIONS = "OCF_parliamentary_parties_1"
				SUPPORT = "[?OCF.OCF_national_support_[FACTIONS]_proportion|2]"
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_[FACTIONS] = [SEAT]
			}
		}
		SEAT = "[?seat_temp]"		#席位
		FACTIONS = "[?factions_temp]"		#派系编号
	}
}

#将增加随机派系支持
OCF_random_region_supports_changes_add = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_random_region_supports_changes_add_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_8 = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#将减少随机派系支持
OCF_random_region_supports_changes_del = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_random_region_supports_changes_del_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_1 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_2 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_3 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_4 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_5 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_6 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_7 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {

		}
	}

#刷新所有地区数据
OCF_refresh_all_regional_data = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_computable_region_triggers = yes
		}
		OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = yes
	}
	OCF_region_supports_formatting = yes
}

#切换党魁
OCF_switching_party_leaders = {
	OCF = {
		set_variable = {
			OCF_party_opened_tab = 1
		}
		#将界面退出
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_show_all_party_leaders = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = token:OCF_Izumi_Sojiro
					}
				}
				add_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = token:OCF_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
					}
				}
				add_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = token:OCF_Kuroi_Nanako
					}
				}
				add_ideas = OCF_idea_Kuroi_Nanako
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF_party_leader_5_variable = OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v
			}
			#定义显示谁
		}
	}
}

#刷新党魁
OCF_refresh_party_leader = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Yasumori_Minori
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Yasumori_Minori
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader_5_variable = token:OCF_Izumi_Sojiro
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader_5_variable = token:OCF_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader_5_variable = token:OCF_Kuroi_Nanako
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Kuroi_Nanako
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Altair
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Altair
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1_yes
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Yasumori_Minori
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Yasumori_Minori
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2_yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3_yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4_yes
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5_yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader_5_variable = token:OCF_Izumi_Sojiro
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader_5_variable = token:OCF_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader_5_variable = token:OCF_Kuroi_Nanako
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Kuroi_Nanako
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6_yes
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Altair
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Altair
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7_yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8_yes
		}
	}
}

			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6_yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6_yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7_yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7_yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8_yes
		}
		clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8_yes
	}
}

#清除所有副领导人 现在这个没必要了，我精神加了自动移除
OCF_clear_all_deputy_leaders = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_idea_parliament
		}
		remove_ideas = OCF_idea_parliament
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Kagami
		}
		remove_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Kagami
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
		}
		remove_ideas = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
	}
}

#选举后重置执政党
OCF_reset_ruling_party = {
	OCF_eliminate_current_ruling_party = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
		OCF_elected_faction_1 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
		OCF_elected_faction_2 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 3
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
		OCF_elected_faction_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 4
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
		OCF_elected_faction_4 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 5
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
		OCF_elected_faction_5 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 6
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
		OCF_elected_faction_6 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 7
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7
		OCF_elected_faction_7 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 8
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8
		OCF_elected_faction_8 = yes
	}
	OCF_party_relations_refresh = yes
}
